                        <div data-reactid="1839">
                         Hotel Boutique Casa Quetzal in the heart of Valladolid, Yucatan. Bed &amp; Breakfast Hotel with spacius rooms, decorated with Mexican handcrafts, Around a beautiful garden and pool, where you can have a relaxing time in Yucatan.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1840">
                         The room is very spacious, it has two double beds, two night tables a desk, two rocking chairs with a coffee table. , 
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1841">
                         We are located right next to the majestic ex convent of San Bernardino de Siena in the historical center; we are 5 blocks away from the main square and walking distance to several restaurants and stores.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1842">
                         <li data-reactid="1843"><p data-reactid="1844">The hotel itself is very nice....but if you come on a off season, it's very possible that you will be left all by yourself during the night. I mean with no single service staff at all, only a phone with some emergency numbers. And that is quite scary if you are in a new place and don't speak the language......</p><span data-reactid="1845">Hongzi</span><span data-reactid="1846">2015-06-13T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1847"><p data-reactid="1848">The best bed and softes sheets in the world. Casa Quetzal was wonderful: clean, relaxing and close to downtown. I really recomend this beautiful colonial place. The room was very spacious as well.</p><span data-reactid="1849">Sandra</span><span data-reactid="1850">2015-09-13T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1851"><p data-reactid="1852">A beautiful little retreat. We spent one night here on our way to Chichen-itza. The inner courtyard was gorgeous and well kept. The rooms were very clean and had a warm feel. We loved the hammock and rocking chairs in our room. We stayed in Room 2 and could hear some traffic noise from the Main Street at night. We loved the simple and healthy breakfast served by kind and smiling staff. The breakfast was a bowl of fresh cut fruit, a basket of warm breads, granola, yogurt, fresh orange juice, and tea/coffee. The check in and check out process was simple and easy to navigate. Secure (locked) car parking and secure front door to the complex. We would say the only drawback is that the main square is much more than 5 blocks away (as per the listing) and after dark did not feel like a safe walk-able distance. We had a car, so it was no problem for us. But someone on foot may not feel as comfortable. Overall, we would definitely stay here agin if in Valladolid. </p><span data-reactid="1853">Pamela</span><span data-reactid="1854">2016-01-05T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1855"><p data-reactid="1856">The room was nice, large, and clean. The decorations throughout were charming and a good location. However, the toilet repeatedly had trouble flushing and was not repaired. While the breakfast was tasty, it was incredibly overpriced and not worth it. Overall, we were disappointed.</p><span data-reactid="1857">Hannah</span><span data-reactid="1858">2014-12-25T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1859"><p data-reactid="1860">This is best hotel we stayed it in all of our travels in Mexico. Casa Quetzal has very friendly staff who put up with my gesticulating-lack-of-Spanish communication mode. The room was spacious, the bed was just a teeny bit cramped for my husband and I, but not overly so. The interior courtyard is tastefully decorated with urns and plants and a pool. The breakfast (for additional charge) is filling, although I think it is possible to get better deal at very close walking distance from here. The GPS had trouble locating this place. Either take directions from (SENSITIVE CONTENTS HIDDEN) maps and/or ask the locals once you get there. The people in this town are some of the friendliest people on Earth! The communication with the host before checking in was a little sketchy and I thought this may not have been the best decision, but they were more responsive closer to the check-in date. Great town to stay in, to visit Chichen Itza and Ek Balam.</p><span data-reactid="1861">K.P. (Suba)</span><span data-reactid="1862">2015-02-23T00:00:00Z</span></li>

There are a lot of things to explore in and around Valladolid, like the Yucatan's many cenotes or the numerous ancient, Mayan sites like Ek Balam or Chichen Itza. The Caribbean Sea and its beautiful beaches is only 1 hour away, and the Golf with Biospheres and flamingoes 1 1/1 up north! We are in between Merida and Cancun, and the Cancun airport is only 1 1/2 hours away.
